 In any Bill, a clause contains a 'statement of Objects and Reasons', detailing why and for what purpose this amendment is being done, but not in this Bill
 Happened
 ek sanyukt sansadeey samiti (JPC) ne is sanshodhan kaa dhai saal tak nirikshan kiya or is saal janvari main report saunpi
 When this committee sought clarification about the purpose of the bill, two things were said by the government: (a) It has been 'mentioned' in the 'cabinet Note' issued for amendment
 (b) grih mantralay ke 2015 or 2016 ke notification main iske bare main bataaya gaya he
 The JPC accepted these explanations without question
 yah hairaani kii baat he ki cabinet note saarvajanik kagajaat nahin hote or unamem die gaye tathyon ke bare main sabko pataa nahin hota,jabaki kanoon main koi bhi sanshodhan hota he to isaki vyakhya or spashtikaran vidheyak ke 'uddeshyon or kaarnon kaa byora' khand main diya jaataa he
 Secondly, the Home Ministry notifications mention only 'religious persecution' to create a new group of beneficiaries
 ye notifications 'passport (entry intu india) 1950 main sanshodhan karke do padosi deshon bangladesh or pakistan se aane vaale chah alpsankhyak samoohon (hindu, sikh, buddha, jain, parsi or isai) ko jodate hai or kehete hai 'ye samooh dharmik utpeedan yaa dharmik utpeedan ke dar se bharat main sharan lene ko majaboor hai
 'it has not been explained on what basis, on the basis of which data or analysis, it has been concluded that certain religious groups of certain countries are being persecuted on the basis of religion and others are not being persecuted

 labhaarthiyon kaa vargeekaran or taarkik vibhed (intelligible Differentia)naagarikta (sanshodhan) vidheyak ke saamne sabase badi chunauti samvidhan ke anuchhed 14 main die gaye samanta ke adhikaar se milegi, jo kahata he, 'rajya bhartiya seemaa ke bheetar kisi ko bhi kanoon ke samaksh samta or kanoonee sangrakshan se vanchit nahin karegaa
 a petition challenging the Citizenship (amendment) Bill is pending in the Supreme Court and this petition will be heard as soon as Parliament passes the bill
 naagarikta (sanshodhan) vidheyak ko is saal janvari main loksabhaa main paas kar diya gaya tha, lekin rajyasabha main yah paas nahin ho sakaa tha

 vibhaag ne bataaya ki is tarah kaa koi ulanghan nahin hota he

 Justice SR Tendulkar case, which focuses on 'the true meaning and prospects of Article 14'
 yah faisla kisi tarah ke vargeekaran main upachaar kii samanta ke liye do purv sharten rakhata he: (i) iskaa aadhaar taarkik vibhed (intelligible differentia) hona chahie, jo kisi bhi labhaarthi samooh main jo rakhe gaye hai or jo nahin rakhe gaye hai, unamem taarkik bhed karata he
 (ii) Whatever distinction is made to achieve this goal, this distinction must have a 'logical relation' to its goal
 JPC ne yah jaanane athwa is par spashtikaran maangane kii koshish nahin kii ki kyon or kaise labhaarthiyon ke samooh main muslimon ko shaamil nahin kiya gaya or kya yah anuchhed 14 kaa bhedbhaavpurn ulanghan nahin he

 yah sarvavidit he ki myanmar main rohingya (is saal janvari main inamen se kuch bangladesh bhej die gaye

 is
